var dataArray = [0,1,2,4,6,8,12,11,11,9,6,3,3,4,6,8,9,8,9,10,11,12,10,8,6,5,3]
var sensitivity = 0.05 * Math.max(...dataArray);
var nPeaks = 0
var iCandidateNumber = -1
var iCandidateValue = -1;
var rCandidateRatingLeft = 0;
var rCandidateRatingRight = 0;
dataArray.forEach((value, number) => 
{ 
    if(value > iCandidateValue) {
        if(iCandidateValue > 0)
            rCandidateRatingLeft += (value - iCandidateValue);
        iCandidateNumber = number;
        iCandidateValue = value;
        return;
    }
    if(value < iCandidateValue)
    {
    if(rCandidateRatingLeft > sensitivity)
    {
        rCandidateRatingRight += (iCandidateValue - value);
        if(rCandidateRatingRight > sensitivity) {
            iCandidateNumber = -1;
            iCandidateValue = -1;
            rCandidateRatingRight = 0;
            rCandidateRatingLeft = 0;
            nPeaks += 1;
        }
        return;
    }
    }
});
console.log('Peaks:'+nPeaks);
